/////////////////Limp and reraise, Call a jam///////////////

//limp
When OpponentsAtTable=1 and InSmallBlind and Raises=0 and (StackSize>=13 or MinOpponentStackSize>=13) and (PairInHand or Hand=AKsuited or Hand=AQsuited or Hand=AJsuited or Hand=ATsuited or Hand=A9suited or Hand=A8suited or Hand=KQsuited or Hand=QJsuited or Hand=QTsuited or Hand=Q9suited or Hand=JTsuited) and not (Hand=55 or Hand=44 or Hand=33 or Hand=22) Call force
//reraise
When OpponentsAtTable=1 and InSmallBlind and BotsLastAction=Call and Raises=1 and BetSize<=3 and (PairInHand or Hand=AKsuited or Hand=AQsuited or Hand=AJsuited or Hand=ATsuited or Hand=A9suited or Hand=A8suited or Hand=KQsuited or Hand=QJsuited or Hand=QTsuited or Hand=Q9suited or Hand=JTsuited) and not (Hand=55 or Hand=44 or Hand=33 or Hand=22) RaisePot force
//Call jam
When OpponentsAtTable=1 and InSmallBlind and Raises=1 and (PairInHand or Hand=AKsuited or Hand=AQsuited or Hand=AJsuited or Hand=ATsuited or Hand=A9suited or Hand=A8suited or Hand=KQsuited or Hand=QJsuited or Hand=QTsuited or Hand=Q9suited or Hand=JTsuited) and not (Hand=55 or Hand=44 or Hand=33 or Hand=22) RaiseMax force

//reraise
